-04- COMMANDS
------------------------------------------------------------

3xForce
-------
3 times, use the skill 'ForceField'

?-RaSou
-------
??? times, use the combo Ragnarok + Sour Mouth.

L?PeSca
-------
Use the combo L.? Pearl + Scar Beam.

MindLov
-------
Use the combo Mind Blast + Love Token.

R-All
-------
Use a random skill targeting allies and enemies alike.

  (2/8 chance each)  Merton, Quake, W Wind
  (1/8 chance each)  Crusader, ForceField

R-Death
-------
Use a random instant-death skill.

  (4/32 chance each)  Doom, Ragnarok
  (3/32 chance each)  Snare
  (2/32 chance each)  Blaster, Cleave, Cokatrice, Raiden
  (1/32 chance each)  Antlion, Break, Condemned, Dread, L.5 Doom, Mind Blast, Odin, Overcast, Roulette, Shoat, Soul Out, X-Fer, X-Zone

R-Drain
-------
Use a random HP- and/or MP-draining skill.

  (2/8 chance each)  Drain, Osmose
  (1/8 chance each)  Empowerer, LifeShaver, Raid, Rasp

R-Geo
-------
Use a random geomancer-type Dance move.
Equal chance of any of the following:
  Antlion, Cave In, El Nino, Elf Fire, Harvester, Land Slide, Plasma, Rage, Sand Storm, Snare, Snowball, Sonic Boom, Specter, Sun Bath, Surge, Wind Slash

RamShel
-------
Use the combo Ramuh + Shell.

Tentacl
-------
Use the skill 'Tentacle'

W-IceRa
-------
2 times, use the skill 'Ice Rabbit'
